`web/templates/pages/category_form.html`:

```html
{{define "category-form"}}
<div class="card bg-base-100 shadow rounded-box p-6 mb-4">
  <h2 class="text-xl font-bold mb-4">
    {{if .Category}}Edit Category{{else}}New Category{{end}}
  </h2>

  <form
    {{if .Category}}
      hx-put="/categories/{{.Category.ID}}"
    {{else}}
      hx-post="/categories"
    {{end}}
    hx-target="#category-form-container"
    hx-swap="innerHTML"
    class="space-y-4">

    {{/* Name */}}
    <div class="form-control">
      <label class="label" for="category-name">
        <span class="label-text">Name <span class="text-error">*</span></span>
      </label>
      <input
        id="category-name"
        type="text"
        name="name"
        value="{{if .Category}}{{.Category.Name}}{{end}}"
        placeholder="Category name"
        class="input input-bordered w-full {{if index .Errors "name"}}input-error{{end}}"
        required />
      {{if index .Errors "name"}}
      <label class="label">
        <span class="label-text-alt text-error">{{index .Errors "name"}}</span>
      </label>
      {{end}}
    </div>

    {{/* Type */}}
    <div class="form-control">
      <label class="label" for="category-type">
        <span class="label-text">Type <span class="text-error">*</span></span>
      </label>
      <select
        id="category-type"
        name="type"
        class="select select-bordered w-full {{if index .Errors "type"}}select-error{{end}}"
        required>
        <option value="" disabled {{if not .Category}}selected{{end}}>Select a type</option>
        <option value="organ"   {{if and .Category (eq .Category.Type "organ")}}selected{{end}}>Organ</option>
        <option value="species" {{if and .Category (eq .Category.Type "species")}}selected{{end}}>Species</option>
        <option value="tissue"  {{if and .Category (eq .Category.Type "tissue")}}selected{{end}}>Tissue</option>
        <option value="stain"   {{if and .Category (eq .Category.Type "stain")}}selected{{end}}>Stain</option>
        <option value="custom"  {{if and .Category (eq .Category.Type "custom")}}selected{{end}}>Custom</option>
      </select>
      {{if index .Errors "type"}}
      <label class="label">
        <span class="label-text-alt text-error">{{index .Errors "type"}}</span>
      </label>
      {{end}}
    </div>

    {{/* Description */}}
    <div class="form-control">
      <label class="label" for="category-description">
        <span class="label-text">Description</span>
      </label>
      <textarea
        id="category-description"
        name="description"
        placeholder="Optional description"
        class="textarea textarea-bordered w-full"
        rows="3">{{if .Category}}{{.Category.Description}}{{end}}</textarea>
    </div>

    {{/* Parent Category */}}
    <div class="form-control">
      <label class="label" for="category-parent">
        <span class="label-text">Parent Category</span>
      </label>
      <select
        id="category-parent"
        name="parent_id"
        class="select select-bordered w-full {{if index .Errors "parent_id"}}select-error{{end}}">
        <option value="">None</option>
        {{range .AllCategories}}
        <option value="{{.ID}}"
          {{if eq .ID $.SelectedParentID}}selected{{end}}>
          {{.Name}} ({{.Type}})
        </option>
        {{end}}
      </select>
      {{if index .Errors "parent_id"}}
      <label class="label">
        <span class="label-text-alt text-error">{{index .Errors "parent_id"}}</span>
      </label>
      {{end}}
    </div>

    <div class="flex gap-2 justify-end">
      <button type="button"
              class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm"
              hx-get="{{.CancelURL}}"
              hx-target="{{.CancelTarget}}"
              hx-swap="{{.CancelSwap}}">
        Cancel
      </button>
      <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary btn-sm">
        {{if .Category}}Save Changes{{else}}Create Category{{end}}
      </button>
    </div>

  </form>
</div>
{{end}}
```

```html
        <summary class="collapse-title text-xl font-semibold">{{.Name}}</summary>
        <div class="collapse-content space-y-4">

          {{/* Top-level section assignments */}}
          {{if .Assignments}}
          <div class="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
            {{range .Assignments}}
            <div class="card bg-base-200 border-l-4 border-primary shadow-sm">
              <div class="card-body p-4 gap-1">
                <p class="text-sm text-base-content/60">Tissue Record #{{.TissueRecordID}}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            {{end}}
          </div>
          {{end}}

          {{/* Subsections */}}
          {{range .Subsections}}
          <details class="collapse collapse-arrow bg-base-200 rounded-box" open>
            <summary class="collapse-title text-lg font-medium">{{.Name}}</summary>
            <div class="collapse-content">
              {{if .Assignments}}
              <div class="grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4 pt-2">
                {{range .Assignments}}
                <div class="card bg-base-100 border-l-4 border-secondary shadow-sm">
                  <div class="card-body p-4 gap-1">
                    <p class="text-sm text-base-content/60">Tissue Record #{{.TissueRecordID}}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                {{end}}
              </div>
              {{else}}
              <p class="text-base-content/40 text-sm py-2">No tissue records in this subsection.</p>
              {{end}}
            </div>
          </details>
          {{end}}

          {{if and (not .Assignments) (not .Subsections)}}
          <p class="text-base-content/40 text-sm">No tissue records in this section.</p>
          {{end}}

        </div>
      </details>
      {{end}}
    </div>
    {{else}}
    <div class="alert alert-info">
      <span>This collection has no sections yet. Use the builder to add structure.</span>
    </div>
    {{end}}

  </div>
</div>
{{end}}
```

`web/templates/pages/slide_viewer.html`:

```html
{{define "head"}}
<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/openseadragon@4/build/openseadragon/openseadragon.min.js"></script>
<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/usnistgov/OpenSeadragonScalebar@master/openseadragon-scalebar.js"></script>
<style>
  #microscope-viewer {
    width: 100%;
    height: calc(100vh - 56px); /* full height minus the top bar */
    background: #111;
  }
  .objective-btn.active {
    background-color: oklch(0.70 0.14 180);
    color: white;
    border-color: oklch(0.70 0.14 180);
  }
</style>
{{end}}

{{define "content"}}
<!-- Top bar -->
<div class="h-14 bg-base-100 border-b border-base-300 flex items-center justify-between px-4 gap-4">
  <div class="flex items-center gap-3 min-w-0">
    <a href="/tissue_records/{{.Slide.TissueRecordID}}/workspace"
       class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm btn-square" title="Back">
      ←
    </a>
    <span class="font-semibold truncate">{{.Slide.Name}}</span>
    {{if .Slide.Preparation.Staining}}
    <span class="badge badge-outline badge-sm hidden sm:inline-flex">{{.Slide.Preparation.Staining}}</span>
    {{end}}
  </div>

  {{if .Slide.IsTiled}}
  <!-- Objective lens switcher -->
  <div role="group" aria-label="Objective lens" class="flex gap-1">
    {{range .Objectives}}
    <button class="btn btn-outline btn-sm objective-btn"
            data-objective="{{.}}"
            aria-label="{{.}}× objective">
      {{.}}×
    </button>
    {{end}}
  </div>
  {{end}}

  <div class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-base-content/60 shrink-0">
    <span class="hidden sm:inline">{{.Slide.BaseMagnification}}× captured</span>
    {{if .Slide.MicronsPerPixel}}
    <span class="hidden sm:inline">· {{.Slide.MicronsPerPixel}} µm/px</span>
    {{end}}
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Viewer area -->
{{if .Slide.IsTiled}}
<div id="microscope-viewer"
     role="img"
     aria-label="Virtual microscope viewer: {{.Slide.Name}}">
</div>

<script>
(function () {
  const dziURL = "{{.DziMetadata.DziURL}}";
  const baseMag = {{.DziMetadata.BaseMagnification}};
  const mpp     = parseFloat("{{.DziMetadata.MicronsPerPixelJS}}") || 0;
  const homeVP  = {{.DziMetadata.HomeViewportJSON | js}};

  const viewer = OpenSeadragon({
    id:                    "microscope-viewer",
    tileSources:           dziURL,
    showNavigationControl: false,
    zoomPerScroll:         2,
    animationTime:         0.5,
    blendingTime:          0.1,
    constrainDuringPan:    false,
    maxZoomPixelRatio:     4,
    visibilityRatio:       0.5,
    gestureSettingsTouch:  { pinchRotate: false },
  });

  viewer.addHandler("open", function () {
    // Scale bar — attach once on open
    if (typeof viewer.scalebar === "function") {
      viewer.scalebar({
        type:            OpenSeadragon.ScalebarType.MICROSCOPY,
        pixelsPerMeter:  mpp > 0 ? (1 / mpp) * 1e6 : 0,
        minWidth:        "75px",
        location:        OpenSeadragon.ScalebarLocation.BOTTOM_LEFT,
        xOffset:         10,
        yOffset:         10,
        stayInsideImage: false,
        color:           "white",
        fontColor:       "white",
        backgroundColor: "rgba(0,0,0,0.5)",
        barThickness:    3,
      });
    }
  });

  // Go home after the first resize event — this is when OSD has
  // actually measured the container and can center correctly.
  viewer.addHandler("resize", function onResize() {
    viewer.removeHandler("resize", onResize); // fire once only
    if (homeVP) {
      viewer.viewport.panTo(new OpenSeadragon.Point(homeVP.x, homeVP.y), true);
      viewer.viewport.zoomTo(homeVP.zoom, null, true);
    } else {
      viewer.viewport.goHome(true);
    }
  });

  // Objective lens switcher
  // Zoom levels are multiples of the fit-to-screen baseline.
  // We map: 4× → 1× (fit), 10× → 2.5×, 40× → 10× relative to fit.
  const objectiveZoom = { 4: 1.0, 10: 2.5, 40: 10.0 };

  const objectives = document.querySelectorAll(".objective-btn");
  objectives.forEach(function (btn) {
    btn.addEventListener("click", function () {
      const mag   = parseInt(btn.dataset.objective, 10);
      const zoom  = objectiveZoom[mag] || (mag / baseMag);
      viewer.viewport.zoomTo(zoom);
      viewer.viewport.panTo(viewer.viewport.getCenter(), false);
      objectives.forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove("active"); });
      btn.classList.add("active");
    });
  });

  // Keep active button in sync on manual zoom
  viewer.addHandler("zoom", function (e) {
    let closest = null, minDiff = Infinity;
    objectives.forEach(function (btn) {
      const mag  = parseInt(btn.dataset.objective, 10);
      const zoom = objectiveZoom[mag] || (mag / baseMag);
      const diff = Math.abs(e.zoom - zoom);
      if (diff < minDiff) { minDiff = diff; closest = btn; }
    });
    objectives.forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove("active"); });
    if (closest && minDiff < 1.0) { closest.classList.add("active"); }
  });
})();
</script>

{{else}}
<!-- Static image fallback -->
<div class="flex items-center justify-center bg-base-200" style="height: calc(100vh - 56px);">
  {{if .StaticImageURL}}
  <img src="{{.StaticImageURL}}"
       alt="{{.Slide.Name}}"
       class="max-h-full max-w-full object-contain" />
  {{else}}
  <div class="text-center text-base-content/40">
    <p class="text-5xl mb-4">🔬</p>
    <p class="text-lg">No image available yet.</p>
  </div>
  {{end}}
</div>
{{end}}
{{end}}
```
